Â Â In response to the trigger signal, the <figure-callout id="42" label="control unit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">control unit</figure-callout> 42 cancels the DMA transfer of the luminance and color difference signals for one screen currently captured from the <figure-callout id="33" label="CCD" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">CCD</figure-callout> 33 to the <figure-callout id="41" label="DRAM" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">DRAM</figure-callout> 41, and is not shown at a shutter speed according to appropriate exposure conditions. Â Â In the playback mode, the <figure-callout id="42" label="control unit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">control unit</figure-callout> 42 selectively reads out the image data stored in the built-in <figure-callout id="47" label="memory" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">memory</figure-callout> 47 or the <figure-callout id="48" label="memory card" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">memory card</figure-callout> 48, and is compressed by a procedure that is completely opposite to the procedure in which data is compressed in the shooting mode by the <figure-callout id="46" label="JPEG circuit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">JPEG circuit</figure-callout> 46. The image data is read to generate a video signal, which is reproduced and output by the <figure-callout id="21" label="display unit" filenames="0004193804-2.png,0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">display unit</figure-callout> 21.

Â Â If the flash mode is the automatic flash mode and the exposure value is such that the flash emission is required, or the flash mode is set to the forced flash mode, and as a result, if the flash is fired, the step C05 is performed. This is judged, and then it is repeatedly judged whether or not the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 is further fully pressed (step C06) and whether it is still half-pressed (step C07). While the respective states are locked, the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 is fully pressed, or waits for the half-pressed state to be released.

Â Â Here, when the half-press operation of the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 is released, this is determined in Step C07, and the process returns to Step C01 again.

Â Â When the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 is fully pressed from the state in which the AF value and the AE value are locked, this is determined in step C06, the AF processing is locked, and the focus lens in the lens <figure-callout id="32" label="optical system" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">optical system</figure-callout> 32 is temporarily cleared. Is moved to a position that becomes a fixed focus corresponding to the focal length at that time, and at the same time, the strobe light emitting unit 6 is pre-flashed by the <figure-callout id="52" label="strobe driving unit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">strobe driving unit</figure-callout> 52 with a light emission amount corresponding to the lock of the AE processing, and in synchronization with this. Image data is obtained by capturing a still image at a fixed focus (step C08). At this time, the amount of reflected light with respect to the light emission amount of the strobe light emitting unit 6 is calculated from the obtained image data.

Â Â In this way, when performing strobe shooting using the strobe light emitting unit 6, the pre-flash is effectively used to obtain a still image at a fixed focus, and a still image by automatic focusing that is captured at the subsequent main flash. Since it is assumed to be stored and stored in a pair, automatic focusing is performed while avoiding wasting power from the power source battery with limited capacity without wasting the light emission drive of the strobe light emitting unit 6. Even when a still image shot with the function activated is unclear due to factors such as `` out of focus &#39;&#39; or camera shake, the still image shot with a fixed focus using pre-flash just before that is sufficiently clear It is very likely that it is a natural thing, avoiding the situation where only out-of-focus images can be obtained at a precious shutter opportunity, and taking and storing still images focused on the desired subject without fail It is possible.

</span>Next, the operation of the above embodiment will be described. <br/> Also in this <figure-callout id="1" label="digital camera" filenames="0004193804-13.png,0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">digital camera</figure-callout> 1, as in other general cameras, the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 has a two-step operation stroke, and the first step is an operation up to about half of the full stroke, generally referred to as half-press. In the operation state, automatic focusing (AF) processing and automatic exposure (AE) processing are executed to lock the respective processing values, and then, as a second stage, full stroke operation, generally referred to as full press It is assumed that an imaging operation based on the operation logic of executing the actual imaging with the AF value and the AE value is performed in the operation state.</span>

Â Â In addition, shooting at a fixed focus (to be referred to as âPF shootingâ in the figure), which will be described later, refers to the focal length position of the zoom lens selected at that time, the ISO sensitivity setting at that time, and the AE value (light quantity). From the look-up table fixedly stored in advance in the ROM in the <figure-callout id="42" label="control unit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">control unit</figure-callout> 42, the focus lens is moved to a predetermined position, and the so-called âsqueezingâ, in which the aperture (F) value and the shutter speed are read and set. Performing shooting in a state called pan focus (PF), which obtains a depth of field over almost the entire range in practice, or by obtaining a certain large depth of field close to it by executing the shooting performed. Point to.

Â Â If the set flash mode is the automatic flash mode, whether or not the flash mode requires the flash from the exposure value locked in the AE process, or the flash mode is set to the forced flash mode. Â Â In this way, when performing strobe shooting using the strobe light emitting unit 6, depending on the user&#39;s selection setting, the pre-flash or the pre-flash is removed and shooting at a fixed focus is executed, and the main flash after the pre-flash is emitted. Since it was supposed to be stored and saved in pairs with still images taken at autofocus, the still images taken with the autofocus function activated as a result of blurring or camera shake, etc. Even in such a case, it is highly possible that a still image captured at a fixed focus using pre-flash just before that is sufficiently clear, avoiding the situation where only a defocused image can be obtained at a precious photo opportunity. By performing simple AF processing and AE processing and continuously driving the <figure-callout id="33" label="CCD" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">CCD</figure-callout> 33 at a high shutter speed in consideration of the frame rate, the state of the through image display in which the content captured by the <figure-callout id="33" label="CCD" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">CCD</figure-callout> 33 is displayed on the <figure-callout id="21" label="display unit" filenames="0004193804-2.png,0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">display unit</figure-callout> 21 is changed. While maintaining (step H01), it is determined whether or not the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 of the <figure-callout id="49" label="key input unit" filenames="0004193804-3.png" state="{{state}}">key input unit</figure-callout> 49 has been half-pressed (step H02), so that the <figure-callout id="9" label="shutter key" filenames="0004193804-2.png" state="{{state}}">shutter key</figure-callout> 9 is in a half-pressed state. Wait for.
</span>

</span>
Â Â Furthermore, scene program shooting, which will be described later, means that shooting is automatically performed with the optimum setting for the shooting scene by selecting one of a plurality of types in which shooting conditions are programmed in advance in shooting mode. For example, &#34;person&#34; &#34;landscape&#34; &#34;landscape and person&#34; &#34;person up&#34; &#34;person bust up&#34; &#34;two shot&#34; &#34;children&#34; &#34;candlelight and person&#34; &#34;party&#34; &#34;pet&#34; &#34;Flower up&#34; &#34;Bright green&#34; &#34;Autumn leaves&#34; &#34;Smooth water flow&#34; &#34;Still water splashing&#34; &#34;Building&#34; &#34;Cityscape&#34; &#34;Blue sky&#34; &#34;Bright sand beach and sea&#34; &#34;Sunset&#34; &#34;Night view&#34; &#34;Night view and people&#34; One of ââ, âfireworksâ, âfoodâ, âcharactersâ, and the like is selected.
</span>
    </p>
    <p>
      <span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">
  å·ä½çãªæ®å½±æ¡ä»¶ã®è¨­å®åå®¹ã¨ãã¦ã¯ãä¾ãã°ãé®®ãããªç·ãã§ããã°ã·ã£ã¼ããã¹ããã¼ããå½©åº¦ãé«ããè²å¼·èª¿ãç·ã«è¨­å®ããããããã¯ãã­ã£ã³ãã«ã©ã¤ãã¨äººç©ãã§ããã°ã·ã£ã¼ããã¹ãã½ããããã¯ã¤ããã©ã³ã¹ãå¤ªé½åãã·ã£ãã¿éåº¦ãéããã¹ãã­ãã¢ã¼ããèµ¤ç®è»½æ¸ã«è¨­å®ããããã¨ã«ãªãã

Â Â Specific settings for shooting conditions include, for example, âbright greenâ, sharpness is hard, saturation is high, color enhancement is set to green, or âcandlelight and peopleâ is sharpness. The white balance is sunlight, the shutter speed is slow, and the strobe mode is set to red-eye reduction.

Â Â Depending on the selected content of the scene program shooting, it is expected that there will be insufficient illuminance such as `` children &#39;&#39;, `` pets &#39;&#39;, `` stopping splashes &#39;&#39; and other subjects moving, `` candlelight and people &#39;&#39;, `` party &#39;&#39;, `` night view &#39;&#39; In many cases, it is difficult to perform an automatic focusing operation and the shooting is likely to fail.

  ã¾ããä¸è¨ã¹ãããï¼«ï¼ï¼ã§å¥æ¿ã®åè£ã¨ãªãç»åãã¼ã¿ãåä¸ãã¼ã¿ãã©ã«ãåã«ã¯ãªãã¨å¤æ­ããå ´åã«ã¯ããã®å¥æ¿ãã®æç¤ºã¯ç¡å¹ï¼ï¼®ï¼¯ï¼°ï¼ã¨ãã¦å¦çããåã³ä¸è¨ã¹ãããï¼«ï¼ï¼ããã®å¦çã«æ»ãã

Â Â If it is determined in step K11 that the replacement candidate image data is not in the same data folder, the replacement instruction is processed as invalid (NOP), and the process returns to step K02 again.
